\index{object\_type@{object\_type}!sysio::chain@{sysio::chain}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{object\_type}{object\_type}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacesysio_1_1chain_a2d924ca9891de9b9edf3ccb582ec7591} 
enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesysio_1_1chain_a2d924ca9891de9b9edf3ccb582ec7591}{sysio\+::chain\+::object\+\_\+type}}}

\doxylink{struct_list}{List} all object types from all namespaces here so they can be easily reflected and displayed in debug output. If a 3rd party wants to extend the core code then they will have to change the packed\+\_\+object\+::type field from enum\+\_\+type to uint16 to avoid warnings when converting packed\+\_\+objects to/from json.

UNUSED\+\_\+ enums can be taken for new purposes but otherwise the offsets in this enumeration are potentially shared\+\_\+memory breaking \begin{DoxyEnumFields}[2]{Enumerator}

\Hypertarget{namespacesysio_1_1chain_a673425e013b1d45337e8e10cdde4e0c5}\index{sysio::chain@{sysio::chain}!filter\_data\_by\_marker@{filter\_data\_by\_marker}}
\index{filter\_data\_by\_marker@{filter\_data\_by\_marker}!sysio::chain@{sysio::chain}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{filter\_data\_by\_marker()}{filter\_data\_by\_marker()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacesysio_1_1chain_a673425e013b1d45337e8e10cdde4e0c5} 
template$<$typename Data\+Range , typename Marker\+Range , typename Marker $>$ \\
Data\+Range sysio\+::chain\+::filter\+\_\+data\+\_\+by\+\_\+marker (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Data\+Range}]{data}{, }\item[{Marker\+Range}]{markers}{, }\item[{const Marker \&}]{marker\+Value}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Takes two parallel ranges, a \doxylink{struct_data}{Data} range containing data values, and a Marker range containing markers on the corresponding data values. Returns a new \doxylink{struct_data}{Data} range containing only the values corresponding to markers which match marker\+Value

For example\+:
